***marshmallow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a> (26586)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mersċmealwe</i>, corresponding to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">marsh</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mallow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallows.html>marshmallows</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A species of mallow, <i>Althaea officinalis</i>, that grows in marshy terrain. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1653</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nicholas_Culpeper" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nicholas Culpeper">Nicholas Culpeper</a>, <i>The English Physician Enlarged</i>, Folio Society 2007, page 180:
<dl><dd>Our common <b>Marsh Mallows</b> have diverse soft, hoary white stalks <a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>rising</a> to be three or four foot high, spreading forth many <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A type of confectionery, originally (since Ancient Egyptian times) made from this plant, but now generally made of sugar or corn syrup, gelatin that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> pre-softened in water, gum arabic, flavorings, and sometimes beaten egg whites, all whipped to a spongy consistency. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span> <i>Love, Life and Work</i>:
<dl><dd>The Disagreeable Girl <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a female of the genus <a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a> persuasion, built around a digestive apparatus that possesses marked <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b> proclivities.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span> PH Wodehouse, <i>A Wodehouse Miscellany</i>:
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an apple <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:sundae.html>sundae</a>, I recollect. I dug my spoon into it with an assumption of gaiety which I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> far from feeling.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> soft and benign.
<dl><dd><i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a> like a total badass, but he's really just a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b> once you get to know him.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b>  <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> sponzig <a href = vnd.unilang:snoepje.html>snoepje</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:volgens.html>Volgens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ulf.html>Ulf</a> Schott, <a href = vnd.unilang:verantwoordelijk.html>verantwoordelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> jeugdbeleid <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duitse.html>Duitse</a> voetbalbond, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> jeugdvoetbal <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b>-experiment’ <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitstel.html>uitstel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> behoeftebevrediging. „Kinderen <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> offers <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdeling.html>verdeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:disciplineren.html>gedisciplineerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:presteren.html>presteren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zowel.html>zowel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> school <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> in sport.” <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***martelaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaar</a> (10272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>This word seems to come from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelen.html>martelen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.
However, it originates from latin <i>Martyr</i>. Between 1201 and 1250 the word <i>martelare</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> in use in Dutch, and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from this word.
The 'suffix' -aar <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not really the common suffix, but an elongation or derivation of the Latin word.
Therefore, a <a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not someone who tortures (<a href = vnd.unilang:martelen.html>martelen</a>), but an actual martyr, who undergoes the torture (<a href = vnd.unilang:gemarteld.html>gemarteld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaars.html>martelaars</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaren.html>martelaren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>martyr</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijdt.html>lijdt</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:sterft.html>sterft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarmee.html>daarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:symbool.html>symbool</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezien.html>gezien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strijd.html>strijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemarteld.html>gemarteld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelen.html>martelen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ares</i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelares.html>martelares</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelares.html>martelaressen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelares.html>martelaresje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:marter.html>marter</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">martre</i>, in turn borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*marthar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*marþraz</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:martini.html>martini</a> (6548)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:martini.html>Martini</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:martini.html>martini</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">martinis</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A cocktail made with <a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a> or vodka and <a href = vnd.unilang:vermouth.html>vermouth</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Will you join us at six <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>’clock for <b>martinis</b>?</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">My boss <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> out on another of his three-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:martini.html>martini</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lunches.html>lunches</a>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sometimes proscribed</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any cocktail served in a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cocktail_glass" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:cocktail glass">cocktail glass</a>, often sweet or fruity and aimed at women.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I love the chocolate <b>martinis</b> at Trendy <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>Bar</a>!</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:massa.html>massa</a> (5065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">masse</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***mastiff.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>mastiff</a> (81558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mastif</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mastyf</i>, an aberrant derivation (with influence from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mestif</i>) from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mastin</i> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mâtin</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*mansuetinus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tamed (animal)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mansuetus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tamed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>mastiff</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mastiffs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One of an old breed of powerful, deep-chested, and smooth-coated dogs, used chiefly as watchdogs and guard dogs.
<ul><li><b>1605</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Lear" class="extiw" title="w:King Lear">King Lear</a></i>, Act III, Scene VI
<dl><dd>Avaunt, you curs! Be thy mouth or black or white, Tooth that poisons if it bite; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>Mastiff</a></b>, greyhound, mongrel grim, Hound or <a href = vnd.unilang:spaniel.html>spaniel</a>, brach or him.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1896</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" class="extiw" title="w:Theodore Roosevelt">Theodore Roosevelt</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ranch.html>Ranch</a> Life and the Hunting-Trail</i>, The Century Co., chapter 11
<dl><dd>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>Mastiff</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a good fighter, and can kill a wildcat, taking the necessary punishment well, as <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> found out when <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> once trapped one of these small lynxes.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mastodont.html>mastodont</a> (68825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mastodonte</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mastodont.html>mastodont</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mastodonten.html>mastodonten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mastodont.html>mastodontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mastodon</span>, mammal of the family Mammutidae, especially of the genus <i>Mammut</i> <span class="defdate">[from 1807]</span>
<ul><li><b>1807</b> April 3, "<a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschappen.html>Wetenschappen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:letteren.html>letteren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunsten.html>kunsten</a>", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:koninklijke.html>Koninklijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>courant</a></i>, issue 80, page 3.

***mat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> mat (7015)</h1><br></body> 
***matador.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:matador.html>matador</a> (29813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:matador.html>matador</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">killer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Used in the English language as title for a bullfighter, however referred to as a <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">torero</i> in Spain.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:matador.html>matador</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:matadors.html>matadors</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:matadores.html>matadores</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en">matadora</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">bullfighting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The person whose aim <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to kill the bull in a bullfight.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A certain game of dominoes in which four dominoes (the 4-3, 5-2, 6-1, and double <a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a>), called <i><a href = vnd.unilang:matadors.html>matadors</a></i>, may be played at any time in any way.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:clubs.html>clubs</a>, or any other trump <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> in sequence with it, in the game of <a href = vnd.unilang:skat.html>skat</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of the three chief cards in ombre and <a href = vnd.unilang:quadrille.html>quadrille</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:matador.html>matador</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:stierenvechter.html>stierenvechter</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> eersten</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">match</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">box</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>A small cardboard box in which <a href = vnd.unilang:matches.html>matches</a> are kept.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the die-cast toy car <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matchbox_(brand)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Matchbox (brand)"><a href = vnd.unilang:matchbox.html>Matchbox</a></a> owned by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mattel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mattel">Mattel</a>, so-called due to the size of the toys to fix in matchboxes.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:matchbox.html>matchbox</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">matchboxes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any small die-cast toy car, usually collectible.</li></ol>

***mateloos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mateloos.html>mateloos</a> (43432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maat.html>maat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">measure, size</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-less</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mateloos.html>mateloos</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mateloos.html>matelozer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mateloos.html>mateloos</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">mateloost</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>immoderate, excessive</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">materiael</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">material</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">material</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">materialis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">materia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wood, material, substance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mater</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***matras.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:matras.html>matras</a> (7743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">matrasse</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">matratse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">materas</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">matelas</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">materasso</i> (cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Occitan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Occitan language">Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc">almatrac</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">almadraque</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">almadraque</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">مَطْرَح‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maṭraḥ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself perhaps from <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">مُطْرَح‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muṭraḥ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:matras.html>matras</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:matrassen.html>matrassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:matras.html>matrasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mattress (a firm <a href = vnd.unilang:pad.html>pad</a> on which a person can recline and sleep)</li>
<li>By extension, a technical bedding or padding to protect something</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A slut, harlot, a girl so easy that 'everybody does her'; sometimes extended to <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> who are promiscuous</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:matras.html>matras</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">مَطَرَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maṭara</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leather bag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***matron.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:matron.html>matron</a> (90836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:matrone.html>matrone</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:matrone.html>matrone</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mātrōna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">married woman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">māter</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">matrona</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:matron.html>matron</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">matrons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mature or elderly woman.
<ul><li><b>1655</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Fuller" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Thomas Fuller">Thomas <a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>Fuller</a></a>, <i>Church-History of Britain</i>
<dl><dd>grave from her cradle, insomuch that she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:matron.html>matron</a></b> before she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a mother</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A wife or a widow, especially, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> borne children.</li>
<li>A woman of staid or motherly manners.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1606</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macbeth" class="extiw" title="w:Macbeth">The <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>Tragedie</a> of Macbeth</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act IV, scene iii], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uNtBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=RA2-PA246">page 146</a>, column 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But there’s no bottome, none / In my Voluptuouſneſſe : Your Wiues, your Daughters, / Your <b>Matrons</b>, and your Maides, could not fill vp / The Ceſterne of my Luſt, and my Deſire / All continent Impediments would ore-beare / That <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> oppoſe my will.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1907</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_W._Chambers" class="extiw" title="w:Robert W. Chambers">Robert William Chambers</a>,  chapter IX, in  <cite>The Younger Set</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D._Appleton_%26_Company" class="extiw" title="w:D. Appleton amp; Company">D. Appleton amp; Company</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/24962326">24962326</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>“A tight little craft,” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> Austin’s invariable comment on the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:matron.html>matron</a></b>; and she looked it, always trim and trig and smooth of surface like a converted yacht cleared for action.  |  Near her wandered her husband, orientally bland, invariably affable,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A housekeeper, especially, a woman who manages the domestic economy of a public institution.</li>
<li>A senior female nurse in an establishment, especially a hospital or school.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:matron.html>matron</a></b> of a school or hospital</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A female prison officer.</li></ol>

***matroos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:matroos.html>matroos</a> (9309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">matelots</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> ("sailors"), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">matenot</i> ("sailor, bunkmate"), most likely from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mattenoot</i> ("bunk fellow") or less likely <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">mötunautr</i> ("food companion").
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:matroos.html>matroos</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:matrozen.html>matrozen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:matroos.html>matroosje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sailor, seaman</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">matrozenbuis</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">matrozenpak</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:matroos.html>matroos</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:scheepvaart.html>scheepvaart</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeeman.html>zeeman</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laagste.html>laagste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rang.html>rang</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mausōlēum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Μαυσωλεῖον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Mausōleîon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Μαύσωλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Maúsōlos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; named for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mausolus" class="extiw" title="w:Mausolus">Mausolus</a> (Μαύσωλος or Μαύσσωλλος), satrap of the Persian empire and ruler of Caria

***mauve.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mauve.html>mauve</a> (46948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">malva</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mallow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a purple colour; ultimately of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semitic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Semitic languages">Semitic</a></span> origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:mauve.html>mauve</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr">mauves</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mallow</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:mauve.html>mauve</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr">mauves</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mauve.html>mauve</a></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:mauve.html>mauve</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr">mauves</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mauve.html>mauve</a></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mauve.html>mauve</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mave</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mǣw</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mew, seagull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maihwaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maiwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seagull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mouette</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Möwe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seagull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meeuw.html>meeuw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seagull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a ***maw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maw.html>maw</a> (103205)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mawe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">maghe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">maȝe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">maga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stomach; <a href = vnd.unilang:maw.html>maw</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*magô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly; stomach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mak-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*maks-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bag, <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a>, belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">mage</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maag.html>maag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stomach; belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de"><a href = vnd.unilang:maag.html>Maag</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:magen.html>Magen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stomach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">mave</i>, 
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">mage</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stomach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">mage</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stomach; belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and also with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">megin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, archaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мошна́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mošná</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pocket, bag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">mãkas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">purse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maw.html>maw</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maws</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The stomach, especially of an animal.
<ul><li><b>1667</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="w:John Milton">John Milton</a>, <i>Paradise <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a>,</i> Book X:
<dl><dd>So Death shall be deceav'd his glut, and with us two / Be forc'd to satisfie his Rav'<a href = vnd.unilang:nous.html>nous</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maw.html>Maw</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The upper digestive tract (where food enters the body), especially the mouth and <a href = vnd.unilang:jaws.html>jaws</a> of a fearsome and ravenous creature.
<ul><li><b>1818</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Keats" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Keats">John Keats</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Endymion_(poem)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Endymion (poem)">Endymion</a></i>
<dl><dd>To save poor lambkins from the eagle's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maw.html>maw</a></b></dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b> November 14,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="w:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>,  chapter 9, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moby-Dick" class="extiw" title="w:Moby-Dick">Moby-Dick; or, The Whale</a></cite>, 1st American edition, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Harper (publisher)">Harper amp; Brothers</a>; London: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Bentley_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Richard Bentley (publisher)">Richard Bentley</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/57395299">57395299</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“I saw the opening <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maw.html>maw</a></b> of hell, With endless pains and sorrows there; Which none but they that feel can tell— <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> plunging to despair.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Any large, insatiable or perilous opening.</li>
<li>Appetite; inclination.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1607</b> (first performance)<b> | </b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Beaumont" class="extiw" title="w:Francis Beaumont">Francis Beaumont</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Knight_of_the_Burning_Pestle" class="extiw" title="w:The Knight of the Burning Pestle">The Knight of the Burning Pestle</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beaumont_and_Fletcher_folios" class="extiw" title="w:Beaumont and Fletcher folios">Comedies and <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Written by Francis Beavmont and Iohn Fletcher Gentlemen. Never Printed before, and Now Published by the Authours Originall Copies.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, London |  Printed for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Robinson" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Robinson">Humphrey Robinson</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Three Pidgeons">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, and for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Moseley" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Moseley">Humphrey Moseley</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Princes Armes in St Pauls Church-yard.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1679, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/3083972">3083972</a></small>, Act 1, scene 1:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>Unless you <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maw.html>maw</a></b> to do <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> good.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
